Petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Rescue Jin Xi

Lawyer Xu Visited Jin Xi at the Japanese Consulate Yesterday

Family Members Determined to Organize a Rescue Group to Fight to the Death

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that in the case of Jin Xi's illegal arrest by the Japanese Consulate, the Municipal Government and the French Consulate have negotiated with the Japanese Consulate. After the Japanese side unreasonably refused to hand him over, Jin Xi's family representatives and legal counsel visited the Japanese Consulate again at 11:00 AM yesterday to inquire about the truth. At 4:00 PM, they visited Secretary-General Yu Hongjun of the Municipal Government to petition for negotiation again. They also stated that the Japanese side's unreasonable obstruction was making the situation increasingly tense. In addition to sending letters to various French organizations and petitioning Foreign Minister Wang to negotiate based on reason, they will also unite with Koreans who have already acquired Chinese citizenship to organize a rescue group to do everything possible to rescue him. The details are as follows:

Petition to the Municipal Government: Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Jin Xi's family representatives Li Shichang and Chen Cijie, along with lawyers Xu Jielou and Yunmei, went to the Municipal Government at Fenglin Bridge to visit Secretary-General Yu Hongjun to request that he promptly lodge a second protest with the Japanese Consul-General so that Jin Xi could regain his freedom as soon as possible. At the same time, they also requested to review the case files of Jin Xi's initial arrest negotiation and the original letters from the French and Japanese Consuls-General to the Municipal Government. The Secretary-General personally received them and showed them the case files and replies. After finally stating their requests, the Secretary-General agreed to immediately submit the case to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for serious negotiation. The representatives were then satisfied and returned.

Inquiry into the Truth: Jin Xi's legal counsel, Xu Jie, went to the Japanese Consulate-General at 11:00 AM yesterday to meet with Ishishe Itaro, the Japanese Consul-General in China, to clarify the truth. After the meeting, he immediately inquired about the reasons for Jin Xi's arrest. The response was that Jin Xi's arrest was related to the bombing of General Shirakawa in Hongkou Park last year and had violated the Japanese law on maintaining public order. After the arrest, a preliminary hearing was held in Shanghai, and he is still being detained at the police station of the Japanese Consulate. Finally, when Lawyer Xu requested to see Jin Xi, the Japanese Consul-General initially refused, but then the police chief agreed to allow a meeting, and they were able to see Jin Xi. However, when the Japanese Consul was asked about the possibility of releasing him, he firmly refused.

Chen Yang's Statement: According to Chen Yang, a representative of the family, who spoke to a Xinsheng News Agency reporter yesterday, after Jin Xi was arrested in the French Concession, his nationality has been completely proven. According to the 1929 Judicial Agreement of the Concession, the French Consulate should be responsible for returning him. According to international private law, the Japanese Consulate's arrest is even more illegal. Therefore, the Chinese and French authorities must lodge a strong protest with the Japanese Consulate and demand his return. Lawyers Lou Yunmei and Xu Jie have carefully reviewed the Shanghai Concession Agreement and international private law. It is believed that the final victory will be based on these two principles. However, this matter is of great importance, and the family's words are weak and light. It seems that it is necessary to have a unified effort from top to bottom, and it may be difficult to overcome the powerful with a weak strategy. Now, in order to concentrate efforts and seek a way to rescue Jin, letters have been sent to various French organizations to form a rescue group, and the law office of Lou Yunmei at 446 Tongdeng Lane, Huage Road, has been designated as the temporary communication address. It is hoped that the wise will guide and assist them as much as possible. Furthermore, since there has been no news of any protest from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, a special petition is submitted to expedite serious negotiation. According to the investigation, there are approximately tens of thousands of Koreans in China, and not a few have already acquired Chinese citizenship. Yesterday, Li Shichang went to various places to report the situation of Jin's arrest to the Koreans, so as to organize a rescue group to fight together.

Letter to Various French Organizations: The family representative's letter to the various French organizations stated: "Greetings. Jin Xi, together with his father Jin Yongduo, naturalized as a Chinese citizen on October 5th, 1929, and executed Permit No. 67 issued by the Ministry of Interior of the National Government. In November of last year, Jin and his father were illegally arrested by the Japanese Consulate, and thanks to the assistance of various French organizations, they were released. Unexpectedly, at around 6:00 PM on November 22nd of this year, he was illegally arrested again by the Japanese Consulate in the French Concession. The representatives have negotiated with the French Consulate according to the law, and the Municipal Government has also lodged a serious protest. More than a month has passed, but he has not been released. The details of the negotiations have been telegraphed to you, which you are aware of. This not only infringes upon personal rights but also damages national sovereignty and international prestige. Therefore, this matter is of great importance, and it is feared that it will be difficult to achieve the final victory without a joint effort. We have always admired your association's upholding of justice and its concern for the interests of the country, society, and the public. We believe that you will definitely sympathize and assist with this case. Since the family's words are weak, we need to concentrate our efforts and have a unified assistance organization to gather strength and make it easier to achieve results. Therefore, we are sending this special letter to request your support. If you agree, please reply by letter or come to discuss and set a date for a meeting so that Jin can be released as soon as possible. The family will be grateful. Jin Xi's family representatives Chen Yangshi and Li Changtong."

Petition to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs: Jin Yongduo, Jin Xi's father, petitioned the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to promptly negotiate seriously with the Japanese Consul-General, stating: "Regarding the petition to lodge a protest, Jin Xi, who naturalized as a Chinese citizen with the petitioner, was arrested by the Shanghai French Concession Central Police Station with the assistance of the Japanese Consulate-General. The petitioner has separately petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Government, your department, and the Shanghai Office, requesting that they forward the matter to your department to lodge a serious protest with the French and Japanese Consulates. For more than ten days, except for the French Consul-General, who has not replied, the Japanese Consul-General has formally replied to the Shanghai Municipal Government, stating that the Japanese government does not recognize that Jin Xi has acquired Chinese citizenship. However, Jin Xi, along with the petitioner, has long since legally obtained Chinese citizenship, and according to Chinese law, Jin Xi should only be recognized as a Chinese national, and his existence as a foreign national outside of China should not be recognized. Moreover, the petitioner and Xi have established their residence within Chinese territory for many years and have nothing to do with Japan in fact. Their jurisdiction should belong to China and should not be infringed upon by the Japanese Consulate-General. Even from the perspective of international private law, even if it is recognized that Jin Xi has an active conflict of internal and external nationality, according to the principles of international private law, even if there is a suspicion of crime, he should be subject to the judgment of Chinese law. The Japanese Consulate-General illegally arrested Chinese citizens, and their whereabouts are unknown. For the sake of protecting the lives of citizens and maintaining national authority, this requires your department to lodge a serious protest with the Japanese Consulate-General. Furthermore, the petitioner and Xi were illegally arrested by the Japanese Consulate-General in the French Concession last year. After the Shanghai Municipal Government protested to the French and Japanese Consulates-General and presented the nationality permit issued by the Ministry of Interior, they were returned by the Japanese Consul-General, and the French Concession authorities released them. The French Concession authorities knew that Jin Xi was a Chinese national in the most important aspect of the relationship. Now, Jin Xi was arrested and handed over with the assistance of the French Central Police Station. The petitioner's representatives, Li Shichang and Lawyer Xu Jie, questioned the French Central Police Station and the French Consul-General, who both claimed that they did not know in advance that Jin Xi had acquired Chinese citizenship. This kind of excuse is obviously to evade the responsibility of violating the 'Agreement on the Establishment of Chinese Courts in the Shanghai French Concession'. Even from the position of the French Consul-General, if it is recognized that Jin Xi has dual nationality, why should only Japanese law be followed and Chinese law be disregarded? Their contempt for our country's national sovereignty has reached its limit. Furthermore, even if the arrest and handover were mistakenly assisted at the time due to not knowing that Jin Xi had acquired Chinese nationality, now that Jin Xi's Chinese nationality has been proven, they should also request his return. Although the French Consul-General notified the Japanese Consul-General, it is not allowed to perfunctorily delay the matter. This requires your department to lodge a serious protest with the French Consul-General and demand the return of Jin Xi. Recently Jin Xi is about to flee to Japan, requesting a prompt separation of the matter to protect the lives of the people and only have empty power, and the sentiment of feeling grateful is at its peak. This is submitted by Wang, Minister of Foreign Affairs of the National Government, and the petitioner Jin Yongduo, residing at 446 Bailaini Mengmalang Road, Shanghai."

United Association of China Cement Factories Petitions for Exemption from Increased Cement Consolidated Tax

Domestic Cement Industry Suffering Deeply in Recent Years

We Request Sympathetic Consideration of Commercial Difficulties and the Rescinding of the Order

The United Association of China Cement Factories in this city states that since the Ministry of Finance implemented an increase in the cement consolidated tax on the 5th of this month, the factories have temporarily endured the pain and paid the tax, but the suffering is indescribable. Yesterday, they submitted a special petition to the Tax Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance, requesting that it be forwarded to the Ministry of Finance to rescind the order and return the additional tax already paid, in order to alleviate the difficulties and maintain the industry. The original petition stated: "Petition for Double Collection of Consolidated Tax, Temporary

Enduring Pain and Paying, Still Requesting the Rescinding of the Order to Maintain Domestic Products and Relieve People's Livelihood. We are in receipt of your department's telegram to Dong Dai, increasing the cement consolidated tax, which was approved by the Executive Yuan meeting proposed by the Ministry and will be implemented uniformly from December 5th of this year. The cement consolidated tax was originally six jiao in national currency per barrel, but now it has been changed to one yuan and two jiao inJia currency. Those packaged in bags are calculated at double the original tax, etc. After receiving the order, the public was shocked. Because the deadline for collection was urgent, the member companies of our association were forced to temporarily endure the pain and pay the tax, but considering the difficulties of the people's livelihood and the dangers of the industry, we dared not resign from trivial matters and explained it to your department in detail. The taxation of domestic cement began in the thirty-third year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty. Domestic customs valued at 5% was collected nationwide. Generally, it was acceptable to collect. It was calculated that each barrel actually collected one qian of Guanping silver, equivalent to one jiao and five fen in national currency. It was not until the sixteenth year of the Republic of China that a surtax of 2.5% was added, which was still only equivalent to two jiao and three fen in national currency. Last year, when the consolidated tax was implemented, it suddenly increased to six jiao in national currency per barrel. Now, not long after its implementation, it has suddenly been doubled, which is compared to the old amount,

Increased Eightfold. Even compared to the sixteenth and seventeenth years, it has increased sixfold, which is truly shocking. Our association clearly knows that this tax can be passed on to buyers, but the amount of the increase is too large, and the deadline is too short. Since receiving the telegram, countless disputes have arisen regarding unfinished civil construction projects and orders that have not been cleared by various companies, and there is no way to resolve them. Moreover, cement is necessary for all public and private construction and is not comparable to luxury goods and consumables. Premier Sun Yat-sen advocated people's livelihood and listed it as the top priority of construction. The Three Principles of the People emphasize housing and transportation. The reason why people can live happily and travel conveniently is entirely dependent on cement. If the tax rate is doubled, it is clear that all transportation will be hindered as a result, which is contrary to Premier Sun Yat-sen's intention to build the country. As far as the member companies of our association are concerned, the domestic cement industry has been suffering deeply in recent years due to the influence of the environment. Although we have been given government recognition of foreign goods import tax to provide protection, due to the frequent domestic affairs and the poverty of the people, they have no time to seek food, let alone discuss construction. Therefore, domestic cement production can only be seen selling in large commercial ports. The inland sales market has recently become increasingly narrow. The national production has always felt that supply exceeds demand. If we

Burdened with Heavy Taxes, then users, except for essential uses, will definitely seek alternatives. It can be asserted that not only will the sales of cement be reduced again, but also, in terms of government tax revenue, it is feared that although the tax rate has increased, the amount of revenue will not be as expected. The result of the investigation only sees that it is merely harming merchants and harming the country's treasury. Furthermore, cement payments are mostly on credit. The consolidated tax is handled by each factory paying in advance, which takes about two or three months. The tax rate is heavy, and the amount paid in advance is even greater. The loss of interest is already unmarketable. If customers go bankrupt, they will have to compensate for the tax in addition to the payment for the goods. All of this suffering cannot be expressed in words. Under the collective discussion of the member companies of our association, it is believed that since the increase and amendment of the tax rate have been ordered and implemented on a deadline, we can only endure the pain and temporarily comply with the payment. On the one hand, we still ask your department to sympathize with the people's difficulties and grant the original case of increased tax

To Rescind the Order, and return the additional tax already paid by various companies in full, to alleviate the difficulties and maintain the industry. We are urgently submitting this petition, and we sincerely hope that your department will review and approve it. We are deeply grateful. Respectfully submitted to the Tax Affairs Department of the Ministry of Finance."

Sino-British Scheduled Communication

Currently Undergoing Correction Work

The International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications is preparing for Sino-British communication. The four large radios, two 20-kilowatt transmitters, and one telephone ordered from the British Marconi Company have been shipped from England to Shanghai. The radio engineers of the bureau supervised the workers and transported the four radios to Liuhe for installation. The two transmitters and one telephone were transported to the Zhenru Radio Station for separate installation. The various projects have been completed in order. The engineers of the station have been actively carrying out correction work in recent days and checking whether there are any errors in the installed machines. According to the person in charge of the station, who spoke to a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, although the construction of the transmitters and radios has been completed, the procedures for line correction are quite complicated. In recent days, engineers have been gathering the applied current in one place and gradually transmitting it to the interior of each machine to start it and test for obstructions. This work is the most complicated and important. It is said that if there is a slight omission during the trial operation of a new machine, it will have a great impact on future communication. Therefore, we must proceed with caution. Once the current can pass through the interior of each machine without obstruction, the second step is to correct whether the sound symbols are clear. The date of the official Sino-British communication must wait until the above projects are completed before it can be determined. According to the current situation, the official communication date will be at the end of January or February next year. This is what the British side can realize. As for the rumor that communication can be carried out on the 10th of next month, it seems difficult to do so in reality.

Telegraph Bureau Messengers Staged a Brief Strike Yesterday

Demanding a Raise, the Authorities Immediately Agreed

Returned to Normal After Only Half an Hour

The Central News Agency reports that the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau messengers of the Ministry of Communications suddenly went on strike at 2:00 PM yesterday to demand a raise. Since Hua Shijian, the director of the bureau's business, immediately expressed his acceptance of the messengers' demands, the turmoil disappeared invisibly after half an hour. The Central News Agency reporter learned the details of the incident as follows:

Delegates Elected: The bureau has a total of sixty-three messengers who work in shifts every day. In previous years, there was a practice of seniority-based salary increases. In July of last year, all the messengers received a general monthly salary increase of two yuan. There was hope for another increase in July of this year, but the Telegraph Bureau did not grant it due to certain reasons. Although the messengers made three requests, they did not get a clear answer. Therefore, when the messengers arrived at the bureau yesterday morning, they held a temporary meeting and decided to elect delegates to make a final request to Director Hua. The delegates elected were Jing Dafa, Xia Shuntang, Yang Zhicheng, Ding Wenhe, and four others.

Brief Strike: At 2:00 PM yesterday, all the messengers gathered in the courtyard of the bureau, and the delegates, Jing Dafa and the other four, requested that Director Hua give a reply to the salary increase issue. Director Hua did not give a concrete reply to the messengers' request. The four delegates were unable to get a clear answer and conveyed this situation to all the messengers. All the messengers, unable to get their request met, announced a strike.

Salary Increase Approved: However, due to the tense situation in recent days, thousands of telegrams have been sent back and forth every day. The messengers' strike had a significant impact. Director Hua, in order to take the overall situation into account, immediately issued an order stating, "The messengers of this bureau will receive a salary increase according to the example of the Wireless Telegraph Station, and I will submit it to the Ministry for approval in the near future, allowing the increase from July of this year." The messengers, seeing that Director Hua had already expressed his acceptance, immediately announced the resumption of work. At this time, it was already 2:30 PM, so the actual strike time was only half an hour. After 3:00 PM, the messengers had returned to delivering telegrams as usual.

Conclusion: According to the messengers' account of the incident, the Ministry of Communications promulgated the Regulations for the Management of Messengers in March of this year, which stipulated performance-based salary increases. Performance is evaluated twice a year, and salary increases are implemented at the end of the year based on the results of the evaluation. Salary increases should have started in July of this year, but although the messengers made repeated requests, they did not get a clear answer. The management regulations promulgated by the Ministry of Communications originally did not distinguish between wired and wireless telegraphs. Now, the messengers of the Wireless Telegraph Station have already implemented salary increases in July of this year, so the messengers of this bureau should also have the same benefits. Therefore, the messengers of this bureau believed that the authorities' refusal to grant a salary increase was inappropriate. However, now that Director Hua has expressed his acceptance, it can be said that this incident has come to a conclusion.

Capital Set at 1.5 Million Yuan

Please Invest Actively

It is reported that preparations have begun and Counselor Yu has been ordered to report the situation in detail within this week so that a decision can be made.

Road Bureau Increases Freight Charges for Bulky and Explosive Goods

The Traffic Departments of the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, yesterday issued a notice to the Traffic Department of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway, the Transportation Section of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway, the Joint Transportation Settlement Office of the Ministry of Railways, the various transportation companies of the two railways, and the station staff of the two railways, stating that upon investigation, loading and unloading workers at various stations have been privately receiving subsidies or setting separate fee amounts for loading and unloading dangerous explosives and bulky goods, due to different working conditions. Although these subsidies are largely voluntary from the shippers, they still violate railway regulations. In light of this, this office has decided to increase the loading and unloading rates for dangerous explosives and bulky goods, and issue clear regulations. At the same time, all illegal subsidies will be rejected. The revised fee rates have been submitted to the Management Bureau for approval under Vehicle Order No. 915. It is now necessary to copy and issue the fee rate table to all for notification, effective from January 1, 1934. Attached is the loading and unloading fee rate table for dangerous explosives and bulky goods (based on actual weight per piece):

Not exceeding 500 kilograms

Exceeding 500 kilograms up to 1,000 kilograms

For each additional 500 kilograms up to 5,000 kilograms

(Bulky Goods) 　　(Dangerous Explosives)

Calculated according to the prescribed rate 　　Collected at double the prescribed rate

Collected at double the prescribed rate 　　Progressively increased according to the prescribed rate

Progressively increased once according to the prescribed rate 　　Can be further increased

For example, if it is 750 kilograms, which exceeds 500 kilograms but does not exceed 1,000 kilograms, the ordinary rate is 2 silver cents per 50 kilograms, and the charge should be 3 silver dimes, doubled to 6 silver dimes, 1 silver dollar and 2 silver dimes. (1,100 kilograms is not exceeding 1,500 kilograms), the ordinary rate is 2 silver cents per 50 kilograms, and the charge should be 4 silver dimes and 4 silver cents, doubled to 8 silver dimes and 8 silver cents, 1 silver dollar, 7 silver dimes and 6 silver cents. (1) If the prescribed rate is 1 silver cent per 50 kilograms, it should be increased by 1 cent. (2) If loading and unloading is done with a crane, it should be calculated according to the prescribed ordinary rate.

Forgery of Lead Coin Making Equipment Uncovered

Lu Ying, the captain of the detective team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently received a tip that someone was privately manufacturing lead coin making equipment at No. 12 Jingshun Lane, Xuxu Road, Nanshi, in the jurisdiction of the Second District of this city, casting and selling them for circulation in the city. Captain Lu, at 7:30 PM yesterday, ordered detectives Xu Youliang, Gu Rusheng, Wang Hongyi, Zhao Jinquan, and Liu Shaoqing, the detective foreman stationed in the district, to lead plainclothes police officers to the aforementioned location, where they uncovered the counterfeit coin making equipment and seized four lead coin molds (printed with versions of Yuan Shikai and Sun Yat-sen), four angular coin molds, 16 lead coins, 45 lead angular coins, and arrested Jiang Yuanfa, 44 years old, from Nanjing; Wu Linchang, 47 years old, from Zhenjiang; Wang Shunlin, 38 years old, from Changzhou; Zhao Shunren, 56 years old, from Nanjing; Ji Zhangshi, 40 years old, from Nanjing; and the second landlord, Zhou Guocai, 34 years old, from Nanjing. Municipal Government Takes Over China Public Hospital

Health Bureau to Take Over Tomorrow

The China Public Hospital in Nanshi was established in October of the Gengxu year of the Xuantong reign of the Qing Dynasty, due to a quarantine crisis in the Shanghai Concession. At that time, public sentiment was anxious and nearly caused a major incident. Later, the hospital was established after negotiations with the Concession authorities for self-quarantine, in order to uphold national sovereignty. It has been in operation for 24 years, specializing in the treatment of infectious diseases such as plague, smallpox, scarlet fever, and diphtheria. Now, the Municipal Government Health Bureau believes that these epidemic prevention matters are the responsibility of the Health Bureau, so it has specially requested approval from the Municipal Government to negotiate with the hospital, with the Health Bureau responsible for managing it, to benefit the citizens. The China Public Hospital convened a meeting of all its directors and decided that epidemic prevention is a matter of local public interest, and decided to lease all its real estate and equipment to the Health Bureau, with the bureau paying an annual rent of 1,200 silver dollars. The Health Bureau has now decided to send personnel to take over tomorrow (the 28th), and has formulated rectification plans and is expanding the internal medical equipment to make it the only municipal epidemic hospital.

Various Lawyers' Associations Oppose Courts Collecting Delivery Fees

Four Points of Opinion Listed

The Shanghai Wu County, Dai Jiang and Jiangning Lawyers' Associations, in order to oppose the courts' collection of delivery fees for service of summons and travel expenses for lawyers handling civil cases, held a joint meeting and decided to nominate the Shanghai Lawyers' Association to draft a document, affix their signatures and seals, and submit it to the Ministry of Judicial Administration requesting the withdrawal of the order. The Shanghai Lawyers' Association appointed a drafting committee, which prepared a draft and submitted it to the Standing Committee for revision and issuance. The document was sealed and sent to the Wu County Lawyers' Association, and then submitted to the Ministry of Judicial Administration. The original text is as follows: A petition to request the withdrawal of the order to collect delivery fees for service of summons to lawyers acting as agents in civil cases. It is based on the instruction of the Jiangsu Higher Court, which in turn is based on Instruction No. 265 of your ministry, which states: Article 158 and Article 243 of the Civil Procedure Law stipulate that lawyers acting as agents in litigation should also be served with summons. The notice that has been used all along is in the nature of a summons, and therefore delivery fees should be collected in accordance with the regulations. Upon receiving this, our associations have learned that your ministry's reference to Article 158 and Article 243 of the Civil Procedure Law is based on the fact that (1) lawyers' notices should not be regarded as summons; (2) lawyers are not parties to the litigation; (3) the rules of the local lawyers' associations stipulate that official letters should be used for lawyers' notices. The Wuchang Lawyers' Association in September of this year and the Wuhu Cangwu Lawyers' Association in October of the same year have submitted documents explaining this matter, so there is no need to repeat it. Now, we will present our humble opinions as follows: (1) The current Civil Procedure Law adopts the principle of party litigation, and does not directly summon lawyers acting as agents. Lawyers in the position of agents are also not directly obligated to be summoned by the same law. From the basic concept of the Civil Procedure Law, lawyers' notices cannot be compared with summons. Moreover, in countries that adopt the principle of mandatory lawyer litigation, notices are used for lawyers acting as agents in civil litigation, and summons are not used, nor is the nature of the notice regarded as a summons (such as the Civil Procedure Laws of Germany, Austria, and Switzerland). From the perspective of the legislative principle of the Civil Procedure Law, it should not be considered that the nature of notices and summons are equivalent. (2) Lawyers are one of the three judicial professions, they wear uniforms in court, and have seats in the courtroom, which is clearly different from the parties to litigation in the Civil Procedure Law. From the perspective of the position of lawyers, lawyers' notices should not be regarded as summons. (3) Since the establishment of courts in China more than 20 years ago, the courts have used notices for lawyers' court dates, and the former Ministry of Justice has specified the format of these notices and specially printed paper for them. It is very clear that their nature cannot be regarded as summons. It is untenable to say that notices are essentially summons. (4) Litigation costs cannot be collected unless they are based on the revised rules on litigation costs. The rules do not explicitly stipulate the collection of delivery fees for lawyers' notices, so the collection is without legal basis, and lawyers should not be obligated to bear the delivery fees. Based on the above opinions, our associations believe that the collection of lawyers' delivery fees is a small matter, but it greatly affects the status of lawyers. Therefore, we urgently submit this statement and attach the documents and telegrams from the Wuchang, Wuhu, and Cangwu Lawyers' Associations, requesting your ministry to review and approve the suspension of the collection of delivery fees for service of summons to lawyers acting as agents in civil litigation, which would be a great favor. Respectfully submitted to the Ministry of Judicial Administration. (Attachments omitted) Respectfully submitted by the Shanghai, Jiangnan, Zhenjiang, Wu County and other lawyers' associations, with their names and seals affixed.

Dredging Bureau Orders Large Offshore Dredger

The Dredging Bureau had previously decided to dredge the Shentan shoal outside the Wusong estuary in response to requests from various Chinese and foreign shipping and transportation companies and the Homing Chamber of Commerce, and had increased the dredging tax, but it has not yet been implemented because the Dredging Bureau's existing dredgers can only dredge the Huangpu River and cannot dredge the offshore area. Therefore, the Bureau's Chief Engineer, Chadley, advertised in European and American newspapers for bids for a self-propelled, trailing suction hopper dredger. A certain German iron factory has been selected to build it, at a cost of over 4 million national currency. It will not be completed until the end of next year, and will sail to Shanghai under its own power. It will begin dredging the Shentan shoal in the spring of the year after next. The Bureau's Director, Song Ziliang, has submitted a report to the government for approval, and it is said that Director Song plans to send Xue, the Deputy Engineer of the Bureau's Mechanical Department, to Germany to supervise the construction of the dredger in order to ensure its perfection.

Rental Vehicles Should Be Submitted to the Ministry of Railways for Approval

Ministry of Railways Instructs Railway Bureaus to Comply

The Ministry of Railways has instructed railway bureaus to comply with the rule that all rental vehicles must first be submitted to the Ministry for approval. The order states: "Due to the impact of years of military conflict, the losses suffered by various railways cannot be calculated. In particular, the lack of vehicles and the repeated damage and loss of vehicles have made it impossible to maintain the current transportation status of the bureaus. Therefore, there are regulations for railway bureaus to rent vehicles to each other to make adjustments, and this has been handled in the past. However, it has been found that there are cases where Railway A rents vehicles to Railway B, or rents them to merchants, without reporting to the Ministry, or even after the contract has been signed. This is not in compliance with the regulations. In the future, when Railway A rents vehicles to Railway B, both railways should first submit all relevant regulations to the Ministry for approval. As for renting vehicles to merchants, the regulations should be carefully drafted and submitted to the Ministry for approval. In addition to separate orders, you are hereby instructed to comply with this order."

Third Lottery of Aviation Bonds to be Drawn the Day After Tomorrow

Fourth Lottery to be Issued as Usual

The third lottery of aviation bonds is scheduled to be drawn publicly at 10:00 AM the day after tomorrow (the 29th) at the Yiyuan in Avenue Albert. All sectors are welcome to attend and observe. The fourth lottery of bonds has already been printed and is scheduled to be drawn on February 28th of next year. The details are as follows:

Drawing the Day After Tomorrow: All procedures for the drawing of this lottery will be the same as for the second lottery. The Ministry of Finance will send a representative to give a speech, but the person has not yet been determined. Zhang Shouyong will not be able to attend due to personal business. According to the local Dayun Company, as of 4:00 PM yesterday, 280,000 bonds had been sold. The company has contracted for 300,000 aviation bonds, which are being distributed in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Sichuan provinces. It is expected that all bonds will be sold out by the morning of the 29th. It is also reported that sales in Beijing have increased.

Change in Drawing Method: The method of drawing the lottery has been changed for the seventh prize. After the first, second, third, fourth, fifth, and sixth prizes have been drawn, the seventh prize will be drawn. The seventh prize has 500 numbers. Another ball will be used for the drawing. The ball contains 500 balls numbered from "000" to "499." The number drawn will be the last three digits of the seventh prize number. For example, if the number drawn is "123," then all bonds with the last three digits "123" will be seventh prizes, and each will receive 200 yuan. All winning bonds can be redeemed at the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications seven days later.

Continued Issuance in the Next Round: According to news from the local Aviation Bonds Office, the fourth lottery of bonds will continue to be issued. The rumor that the issuance will be suspended is completely inaccurate. When reporters visited the office yesterday, they saw that the fourth lottery of bonds had already been completely printed and was being packaged and inspected. It is scheduled to be drawn at the Yiyuan at 10:00 AM on February 28th of next year.

He handed the key to the safe deposit box to his concubine Shi to retrieve items. He also changed the account name to his wife Zhou Likai at the Zhongnan Bank. Recently, Li's condition gradually worsened, and as he was on the brink of death, Li's wife Zhou, in order to organize the family affairs, asked Shi about the items stored in the safe deposit box and invited Shi to open the box and inspect them together. Shi initially prevaricated and was evasive, but after repeated urging, Shi left home without saying goodbye. Later, Zhou invited Li's sister and brother Li Jun to rush to the Zhongnan Bank to open the box and inspect its contents.

Trial Opens for the Zhang Bingqian Slaying Case

Murderers Zhou Gougou and Chen Jinfa Still Trying to Shirk Responsibility

Family of the Deceased Brings Private Suit Seeking 7,000 Yuan in Damages

The Deceased's Aged Mother Also Appeared in Court Yesterday

Zhang Bingqian, a native of this county, lived in Yinxiang Port and was a street paver. On the afternoon of November 18th this year (i.e., the first day of the tenth month of the lunar calendar), he was hacked to death by two companions, Chen Jinfa and Zhou Gougou, with knives. Afterwards, the responsible police station apprehended the two murderers, Chen and Zhou, and handed them over to the local court. Prosecutor Yang interrogated them once, decided to place Zhou Gougou in shackles, and separately detained Chen Jinfa. He went to the scene, verified the corpse, confirmed that he had been hacked to death with knives, filled out the forms, and ordered the corpse to be coffined and buried, pending further investigation. It is now learned that this case has been preliminarily reviewed and determined that Zhou Gougou and Chen Jinfa are jointly guilty of violating Article 282, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, in accordance with Article 253, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Procedure Law, a public prosecution has been filed. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Luo Renji specially opened the Third Tribunal for trial. The court appointed lawyer Hu Yuanjun to defend the two defendants, Zhou and Chen. The family of the deceased retained Zhang Bao-

Tang as their lawyer to request

Private Suit for 7,000 Yuan The judge took the bench and ordered Chen Jinfa, age 33, a native of Shanghai residing at No. 20 Lu Bridge, Yinxiang Port, and a drain worker (i.e., street paver), to be brought to the dock. (Question) Did you kill Zhang Bingqian? (Answer) I did not kill him. At that time, I was already asleep at home. The deceased's nephew, Lin Sheng, came to knock on the door. After I got up and opened the door, they dragged me away, saying that I killed someone. But I returned home from Shanghai on that day (i.e., the first day of the tenth month). Passing through Yangjiabang, I saw Zhou Gougou eating tea in a stove shop there. He asked me if my life was good. I answered that it was not yet finished. At that time, Zhang Bingqian was also sipping tea nearby. Zhang asked me who asked you to do this job. I answered that it was a person surnamed Zhou who was in charge and asked me to do it. Zhao Wei-xian Sues Wei Ting-rong Case

Wei Requests Postponement Due to Illness

Zhao Wei-xian, a native of Henan, previously hired a lawyer to file a complaint with the Second Special District Court, accusing Wei Ting-rong, the former commander of the Chinese Volunteer Corps in the French Concession and a director of the French Municipal Council, and his son Wei Yuan-sheng of false accusation, kidnapping, and ransom. The court had previously summoned them once, but because the French Concession authorities, based on the latter part of Article 12, Paragraph 2 of the Convention, appointed a lawyer to attend the litigation, it was ordered to wait for instructions from a higher level before summoning them again. Yesterday afternoon, it was time for the continued trial, and the details have been reported in the newspapers. It is now learned that the defendant was temporarily unwell due to a cold, so he entrusted a lawyer to request a postponement. The court approved the request, so the court did not open yesterday afternoon and will wait for the court to set another date for summoning and hearing.

Xiang Hai Confectionery Factory Opens New Branch

Candy is a daily necessity, and in recent years, with the increasing number of Chinese people who enjoy it, the number of foreign imports has been very large. Domestic candies are often not well researched, so upper-class people do not hesitate to pay high prices and only favor foreign goods. The Xiang Hai Machine Confectionery Factory in this city is purely Chinese-owned. It has various new-style machines and uses scientific methods to refine high-quality candies. The products are beautiful and hygienic, and the selling price is also quite low. They have already become popular in China, which can resist foreign goods. The factory has expanded its business and specially established a distribution center in the National Goods Market in Sanyuanfang, Hangzhou, and a retail department in the Central National Goods Department Store on Nanjing Road in this city, so that people in Shanghai and Hangzhou can easily purchase them. It is expected that good domestic products will be more popular and can reduce one source of outflow.

A Son of Wealth Studies Aeroplanes In France And Goes Ashore In Hong Kong Halfway.

The Absurd Behavior of Wan Junyao, A Wealthy Playboy.

Abandoning Father and Loving Wife to Live with Two Dancing Girls

—His Wife, Zhang Weizhen, Has Already Sued For Divorce—

Wang Zijing, a compradore of a certain foreign firm, lives at No. 20 Lian'anfang, Yuyuan Road, West Shanghai, and has assets of 400,000 to 500,000. His son, Junyao, is 21 years old. On October 4th of last year, he married Zhang Weizhen as his wife. They are both the same age, so their feelings have become closer after marriage. Wang Zijing is pleased to have such a fine son and daughter-in-law. Unexpectedly, Junyao's will is extraordinarily weak. He likes to frequent dance halls and song theatres, and is easily susceptible to bad influences. Before long, he abandoned his beautiful wife and formed an inextricable bond with a famous dancing girl who was the protagonist in the previous case of Tong Sanmao's love suicide. Their love is deep and their happiness is great. Soon he felt that the strict restraint of his father and the gentle persuasion of his wife at home made it impossible for him to do what he wanted. Therefore, on February 28th of this year, he used the excuse of going to France to study aviation skills in order to serve the country in the future. He asked his father to allow him to study in France. Seeing that his beloved son had such great aspirations to ride the wind and break the waves, Zijing of course agreed and immediately granted his request. His wife, Zhang Zhuzhen, hoped that her husband would become famous and also provided eight hundred and fifty yuan as travel expenses. Who knew that Junyao, after receiving the money, still felt that the amount was small and difficult to spend for a longer period of time. He took the opportunity to steal a diamond ring weighing more than two carats from his wife's dowry. So, the family said goodbye and shook hands with each other. Then, Junyao had a pre-existing scheme. When the ship arrived in Hong Kong, he suddenly went ashore and changed to another ship to return to Shanghai. He rented a house with his lover and lived together. As time passed, the matter was revealed. His father felt deeply distressed, but there was nothing he could do. His wife allowed him to not return. Until May, Junyao suddenly said that his love with the dancing girl had broken down and that they were not like lovebirds, but like swallows separating. Although they had a son, they abandoned them like rubbish. The dancing girl was like a dream.

Letter

Sir, I have read the news item published in your newspaper on the 23rd of this month about the Cotton Control Association stabilizing yarn prices. The section on continuing to release new yarn mentioned that a certain factory continued to release 8,000 bales of secondary yarn. According to the discussion at that time, only new yarn was to be released, and there was no mention of secondary yarn. The content of the manuscript is also inconsistent with the title, which is probably a slight misunderstanding in the interview, resulting in a slight difference. I am sending a special letter to you and ask that you please publish it in the letter column and correct it to show the facts. I will be very grateful. Sincerely, The National Economic Council Cotton Control Association, December 26th.

Incoming Correspondence

Next Year's Plan for Railway Business and Intermodal Transportation

Since Mr. Yu Yanyan, Director of the Business Department and Director of the Intermodal Transportation Department of the Ministry of Railways, was ordered last summer to serve as the Director of the Business Department and Director of the Intermodal Transportation Department of the Ministry of Railways, he has been planning day and night, striving to reorganize railway business and intermodal transportation. There should be a plan for reorganizing national railway business and intermodal transportation, in order to have comprehensive regulations and implement them step by step. It is divided into four parts: business, transportation, intermodal transportation, and personnel. The focus of attention is: in terms of business, how to increase transportation business; in terms of transportation, how to increase transportation capacity to bear the increased transportation business; in terms of intermodal transportation, how to increase transportation business on the one hand and increase transportation capacity on the other hand; in terms of personnel, how to make the implementation of the above methods as beneficial as possible. In other words, the business, transportation, and intermodal transportation departments all focus on "methods of governance," while the personnel department focuses on "governing people," because "methods of governance" and "governing people" must be combined before things can be done. For more than a year, with the guidance of the Vice-Minister and the assistance of colleagues, many of the plans have been implemented in order of urgency, and the results are gradually becoming apparent. If given more time, all other reorganization plans will not be difficult to implement and achieve results. Here are the main points of this plan, which I would like to inform the people of the country. This is Mr. Yan's plan for the coming year.

(A) Complete the Responsible Transportation of Goods by National Railways. All railways in the world are responsible for transportation. This is a matter of course and nothing special. However, the railway transportation in our country is actually the responsibility of the merchants themselves, which causes suffering for merchants, all kinds of malpractices, and almost endless impact. I have often thought to myself that if we talk about improving railway business today, there is no other more urgent plan than organizing responsible transportation. Therefore, at the beginning of my tenure, I made organizing responsible transportation my sole urgent task. In May of the 21st year, I presented a proposal to organize a Goods Responsible Transportation Committee and formulate various regulations. On September 1st of the same year, the Jinpu, Jinghu, and Huhangyong lines were the first to implement it. Subsequently, the Longhai, Jiaoji, Beining, Pinghan, PingSui, Xiang'e, Zhengtai, Daoqing, and Nanxun lines also implemented it one after another. Merchants found it convenient, and freight transportation was revitalized. Although responsible transportation has been implemented on various lines, given the closed-mindedness of our people and the deep-rooted habits of various lines, it is impossible to achieve perfect implementation and thorough reform overnight. Therefore, it is planned to urgently seek a second step of improvement, in order to reach the best possible realm and achieve the completion of responsible transportation. The improvement plans are roughly as follows: (1) Guide freight merchants. The railway is a transportation provider, and its counterpart is the freight merchant who needs transportation. To improve railway transportation, it depends on the efforts and cooperation of both parties. Because railway transportation has not been responsible in the past, few freight owners in our country directly trade with the railway. All goods are entrusted to transshipment merchants to handle. As a result, they lack transportation knowledge and a small number of unscrupulous transshipment merchants take advantage of this opportunity to extort money in addition to legitimate expenses, causing freight owners to suffer all kinds of pain without knowing what to do. Freight owners should consider whether it is more economical to entrust the railway directly or indirectly, depending on the quantity and frequency of the goods they ship. Transshipment merchants should try their best to make it convenient for freight owners, solicit business for the railway, and ensure that both freight owners and the railway are economical. Only then can they survive and develop, and fulfill their responsibilities in the entire national economy. It is planned to select competent personnel from each line, send them to relevant cities, market wharves, and rural areas, and use written or oral methods to vigorously publicize the benefits of responsible transportation, the procedures for consignment and receipt, and the responsibilities of freight owners, transportation merchants, and the railway, so that freight owners and transportation merchants can understand how to strive for transportation convenience and economic costs, and seek business development in the general economic trend. (2) Train railway employees. The completion of responsible transportation depends on the cooperation of freight owners and transportation merchants, but if railway employees still regard themselves as government agencies and act arrogantly, or do not understand the various rules of responsible transportation, or are negligent or delay the acceptance and storage of goods, it will be enough to hinder the development of responsible transportation. Therefore, employees at all railway stations must be trained to make their work scientific and their services commercialized. It is planned to select competent employees from each line, train them first, and then let these employees train other employees, or send those who already have a considerable understanding and experience of responsible transportation to train at various stations. In addition to providing them with knowledge training, they will also be given spiritual and moral training to ensure that they are loyal to their duties and fulfill their duties. (3) Implement inspection methods. The above two methods are all positive plans to complete responsible transportation, but methods must also be formulated to eliminate old habits and prevent new malpractices, so that inspections can be carried out. This inspection method is divided into three types: one is accounting audit, one is vehicle inspection, and one is the dispatch of personnel by the Ministry at any time for secret inspection. The detailed methods will be formulated and implemented immediately. (To be continued)

Educational News from Other Places

Ministry of Education Inspector Zhou Bangdao Discusses the Current Situation of Education in Shaanxi

After returning to Beijing from inspecting education in Shaanxi and Henan, Ministry of Education Inspector Zhou Bangdao is compiling a detailed report on his inspection of education in the two provinces. The following is a preliminary account of the education situation in Shaanxi as discussed by Inspector Zhou in a private conversation.

(1) General Situation: Due to years of famine and banditry in Shaanxi Province, rural areas have gone bankrupt, and society is disturbed. The education cause has been repeatedly suspended in the past few years, suffering great losses. Students' thoughts are extreme, and the academic atmosphere is unusually arrogant. Strange dramas such as expelling teachers and beating principals are often heard. In recent years, the harvest of farmland has been slightly better, and society is more stable than before. The Department of Education has also earnestly focused on rectification. Therefore, various types of education have a spirit of renewal and restoration. Students are also gradually returning to the right track.

(2) Education Funding: The amount of education funding in the province is very small. This year's provincial education funding totals 921,378 yuan, of which more than 102,000 yuan is allocated to educational administration, more than 348,000 yuan to middle schools, more than 192,000 yuan to normal schools, more than 84,000 yuan to vocational education, more than 119,000 yuan to elementary education, and more than 73,000 yuan to social education. Generally, 80% is distributed. In addition to more than 100,000 yuan in Nanzheng County and more than 80,000 yuan in Chang'an County, most of the other counties have 4,000 to 5,000 yuan to 7,000 to 8,000 yuan for education funding.

(3) Educational Institutions: Schools and social education institutions at all levels in the province include: (1) "Middle Schools": Provincial schools include Xi'an High School, No. 1 Middle School, Zhongshan Middle School, Fengxiang No. 2 Middle School, Sanyuan No. 3 Middle School, No. 1 Girls' Middle School, Nanzheng No. 5 Middle School, Yulin No. 6 Middle School, and Ankang No. 7 Middle School, for a total of nine schools (No. 4 Middle School has been suspended). There are also six county-run schools, two joint schools, and six private schools. (2) "Normal Schools": Provincial schools include Xi'an No. 1 Normal School, No. 1 Girls' Normal School, Dali No. 2 Normal School, Nanzheng No. 5 Normal School, No. 2 Girls' Normal School, Ankang No. 7 Normal School, and Yulin No. 3 Girls' Normal School, for a total of seven schools. (Nos. 3, 4, and 6 Normal Schools have been suspended.) There is also one provincial elementary school teacher training center and twelve county-run normal school training courses. (3) "Vocational Schools": Provincial schools include Xi'an No. 1 Vocational School and Sanyuan No. 3 Vocational School (No. 2 Vocational School has been suspended). There are also two county-run schools, one joint school, and one private school. (4) "Elementary Schools": There are six provincial complete elementary schools, 5,458 county-run junior elementary schools, 117 senior elementary schools, 125 complete elementary schools, 3,545 private junior elementary schools, 12 senior elementary schools, 44 complete elementary schools, and 47 public and private kindergartens. (5) "Social Education": Public social education institutions include eight public education centers, 60 libraries (and one private), 754 public schools, 72 reading rooms, 41 gymnasiums, and 75 lecture halls.

(4) Personnel Treatment: The treatment of education personnel is very low. Provincial schools issue 80% of their salaries and then deduct 10% (Shaanxi Provincial Bank notes), and they cannot be received on a monthly basis. The salary amount of county schools is very small, and there are also many discounts and arrears. Private schools live within their means and pay by the hour. The monthly income is often not enough to maintain personal life. The director of the Education Department receives a monthly salary of 120 yuan, and the secretary section chief and inspector receive 80 to 100 yuan per month. With the discount on paper money, the income is meager, but the spirit of service has not diminished because of this, which is commendable.

(5) County Educational Administration: Only ten counties in the province retain county education bureaus. Those that have been abolished are handled in two ways: one is to set up an education assistant in the county government, and the other is to have a certain section of the county government handle it concurrently. Because there is no dedicated person in charge, the efficiency of educational administration is extremely low. For example, the various school laws and regulations recently promulgated by the Ministry have not been transferred to the schools. To revitalize and popularize education, it is necessary to restore the education bureau first.

(6) Elementary Education: There are still senior elementary schools established independently, which is very inappropriate. Those that use the old name of model or the new name of experiment are actually no different from ordinary elementary schools. The first phase of compulsory elementary schools and short-term elementary schools are only run in one or two counties. The provincial and county elementary schools in Chang'an City are doing well, but the provincial elementary schools are more affected by politics, and some facilities are not as good as county elementary schools.

(7) Secondary Education: The provincial middle schools have now been reorganized, and the service spirit of the faculty and staff and the learning spirit of the students are commendable. However, the educational equipment is extremely simple. Except for the senior high school, most of the physics and chemistry instruments and medicines were purchased ten years ago. Due to military and banditry and other influences, there are few remaining. The senior high school inherits the Northwest University and Zhongshan University. The school buildings are spacious, the equipment is sufficient, and the teachers are relatively good. It is worthy of being a leading school in the province. No. 1 Middle School, No. 2 Middle School, No. 3 Middle School, and Zhongzhong Middle School are doing well, and the students have good discipline. The students of the private Rose Girls' Middle School have excellent achievements in drawing and embroidery, but the faculty and staff are too old-fashioned and relatively backward in terms of new education facilities. The private Xianlin Middle School has a long history and a quiet environment. The achievements of production education are unmatched by general middle schools, but the student movement seems to be not very well organized recently.

(8) Normal Education: According to what I saw at the No. 1 Normal School and No. 1 Girls' Normal School, the provincial normal schools are doing a serious job. However, the junior high school classes are more than the normal school classes, which is not in line with the original intention of establishing normal schools. The elementary school teacher training center is for each county to send two to three incumbent elementary school teachers to the center for one semester of training, and then return to the county to serve. The first phase is limited to the counties in Guanzhong, the second phase is Shaanan, and the third phase is Shaanbei. The plan is good, and the implementation is quite spirited. The term of the normal school training courses in various counties is one or two years, which is too short. The equipment, curriculum, and teachers are also inadequate.

(9) Vocational Education: The provincial No. 1 Vocational School runs agriculture, forestry, reclamation, and animal husbandry courses, and the No. 3 Vocational School runs weaving and dyeing courses. The school buildings are spacious, and the farms and factories are large. However, most of the graduates become elementary school teachers or army scribes, and there is no way out for the profession they have learned. The products of weaving, dyeing, and sewing at the Xi'an Private Civilian Women's Vocational School are excellent. Students can earn several yuan a month in remuneration. The school is small in scale, but it is pragmatic and gradually expanding, and it has made many contributions to women's occupations. The Huayin County Weaving and Dyeing Factory has now been changed to a vocational school and a remedial school. The foundation is very good. It is also appropriate to run a factory first and then a school. The person in charge, Li Zhonggui, invented many spinning and weaving machines, which are cheap and beautiful, and greatly contribute to the promotion of vocational education. The Yulin Gongli Shaanbei Vocational School has a long-standing reputation. The various products displayed in the Xi'an Public Education Center are also exquisite. It is said that Inspector Zhou received a telegram from the school in Xi'an requesting him to go there, but due to transportation and time constraints, he did not visit.

(7) Social Education: The Xi'an Provincial Public Education Center is conveniently located, the buildings are neat and elegant, and the layout and equipment are quite complete. All kinds of work are also quite tense. The Provincial Library has spacious buildings and a rich collection of books. The collection of books includes integrated collections, Tibetan scriptures, and works by philosophers from Qin, many of which are rare treasures. The Department of Education has set up dozens of public schools in Xi'an, distributed in different districts, and each district has an experimental public school to lead and coordinate, which is managed and carried out by the Public School Management Office with considerable success. Social education in various counties is mostly nominal due to the knowledge, ability, and sense of responsibility of the people who run it.

(11) Local Education: Inspector Zhou said that among the counties he visited, Chang'an was the best, followed by Sanyuan, Huaxian, and Weinan. Sanyuan County has financial difficulties, but the school staff are diligent, self-sacrificing, and dedicated to public service. Their enthusiasm and perseverance are commendable. There is only one complete elementary school and one junior elementary school in Wugong City. The school buildings and equipment of the former are still considerable, while the latter is not much different from ordinary private schools. Fengxiang lacks normal school talents, so although there are several elementary schools, the results are not very good. Huayin is holding a competition and examination for all subjects in all elementary schools, which is similar to the semester final examination. The education assistant is in charge of the work with great enthusiasm.

Ministry of Education Regularly Convenes Meeting of Public Education Committee

The meeting is scheduled to be held for three days starting on January 11th.

There are a total of 18 committee members and 9 agenda items.

The Ministry of Education invited many public education experts to the Ministry in February of this month to hold a meeting to discuss the implementation plan of public education. After that, it issued an order to all provinces and cities to establish their respective provincial and municipal public education committees. According to the reports received by the Ministry, all provinces and cities in the country have been formally established one after another. However, the members of the Public Education Committee of the Ministry of Education have been appointed for a long time, but because the draft of the public education plan has not been drafted in detail and completed, it has been delayed for a long time. It is heard that the Ministry of Education has now drafted nine plans including the method of promoting public education. Yesterday, the Social Education Department printed and sent them to the education departments of fourteen provinces and cities, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, Anhui, Henan, Jiangxi, Hubei, Hunan, Hebei, Guangdong, Beijing, Shanghai Qingdao, Beiping, etc., to ask them to sign and comment on their opinions and send them to the Ministry before January 8th. And send letters to experts such as Chen Lijiang and Li Zheng to seek opinions on the draft, so that they can be submitted to the Public Education Committee for discussion.

Meeting Schedule: The first meeting of the Public Education Committee of the Ministry of Education has been scheduled to be held at the Ministry of Education at 9:00 am on January 11th. The meeting period is scheduled for the 11th, 12th, and 13th, three days. Yesterday, the printed public education draft and meeting notice were sent to all committee members, asking them to sign and comment on the draft, or if they have any proposals, they must be sent to the Ministry before January 8th in order to compile the agenda.

List of Committee Members: Central Party Headquarters representatives Chen Lifu, Wang Qi, Ministry of Interior Wang Xianqiang, Ministry of Industry Xu Tinghu, Ministry of Education Duan Xipeng, Qian Changzhao, Director of the Social Affairs Department of the Ministry of Education Zhang Jiong, Peng Baichuan, Zhong Lingxiu, directors in charge of the Social Affairs Department, Counselor Chen Panzao, Inspector Zhong Daozan, experts and committee members hired by the Ministry of Education Niu Yongjian, Chen Jianxiao, Meng Xiancheng, Liang Shuming, Gao Jianxi, Yan Yangchu, Xiang Jutan.

Nine Agenda Items: (1) Method of promoting public schools, (2) Draft regulations for public schools, (3) Draft amendments to the temporary regulations for public education centers, (4) Regulations for the Public School Curriculum Standards Compilation Committee, (5) Case of compiling and reviewing public reading materials, (6) Draft method of promoting vocational remedial education, (7) Case of improving and enriching national libraries, (8) Draft regulations for the appointment and treatment of social education personnel, (9) Draft regulations for public education areas in provinces, cities, and counties.

Ministry of Education Urges Provinces to Report Standards for Secondary School Funding

The Ministry of Education previously formulated standards for the equipment and funding distribution of secondary schools, with vocational schools accounting for 40%, ordinary middle schools 35%, and normal schools 25%. It issued an order to all provinces and cities to follow the standards, prepare implementation plans, and submit them to the Ministry for verification by the end of this year. At present, the Ministry of Education has only received the plans from six provinces and cities, including Shanxi, Suiyuan, Hubei, Hunan, Shanghai, and Qinghai. The remaining provinces and cities have not reported. The Ministry of Education has urged the provinces and cities that have not yet reported to submit them to the Ministry by the end of this month as before.

Zhejiang Province's Measures for the Custody and Payment of Special Education Funds

Before Zhejiang designated the custody of special education funds, the receipt and payment procedures were in accordance with the unified receipt and expenditure relationship of the province's finances, and the Finance Department allocated funds on a monthly basis. Although the provincial treasury has always been extremely difficult, the Finance Department has been able to allocate funds to provincial education institutions as a priority. This time, Inspector Dai Xia, dispatched by the Ministry of Education, came to the province to assist in planning the independent education funding in the province. Now the measures for the custody and payment of special education funds have been discussed and approved by the provincial government and reported to the central government for approval and record, and will be implemented accordingly. In the future, the funding of various education institutions in the province will be more guaranteed and stable. The province's education funding totals 2,106,436 yuan. Now it is decided to implement the measures for the custody and payment of special education funds. The important points are as follows:

(1) Designate foil business tax, 1.2 million yuan per year, the full amount of tobacco and alcohol surtax, about 200,000 yuan, and the full amount of slaughter business tax, about 600,000 yuan, for a total of about 2 million yuan.

(2) The aforementioned three tax revenues will be allocated to the province's special education funds and implemented in three phases. In the first phase, the foil business tax will be allocated 90,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.08 million yuan per year, starting in November of the 22nd year. In the second phase, the foil business tax will be allocated 100,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.2 million yuan per year, and the tobacco and alcohol tax will be 200,000 yuan per year, for a total of 1.4 million yuan, starting in July of the 23rd year.

In the third phase, the foil business tax will be allocated 100,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.2 million yuan per year, the tobacco and alcohol surtax will be 200,000 yuan, and the slaughter business tax will be 600,000 yuan, for a total of 2 million yuan, starting in May of the 24th year. The foil business tax in this article should be allocated to the special education funds on a monthly basis as a priority. Before the designated amount for the month has been allocated in full, it shall not be used for other purposes.

Shanghai County Seventh Education Administration Council Winter Meeting

Decided to Establish Chenxing Agricultural Education Center in the Fifth People's Education District

Recommended Members to Draft Next Year's Education Center Plan

Suspension of Sanlin Kindergarten and Transfer of Funds to Free Education

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held the inaugural meeting of the reorganized seventh session of the Education Administration Committee and the winter meeting at 10 a.m. yesterday. Attendees included Pan Zhongjia, Qin Yanqi, Yao Huiquan, Zhang Yi, Chen Pingyi, Zhang Jingye, Shi She, Zhu Hange, Jia Foru, Niu Changyao, etc. Observers included Zheng Yi and Yang Chunlin. County Magistrate Pan chaired the meeting, with Pan Sansheng as the recorder. The meeting began with ceremonial proceedings. First, the chairman read the resolutions of the previous session, followed by the Education Bureau Director's report on the bureau's operational status, economic income and expenditure, the reported status of the 20th year's final accounts, and other important official documents. Subsequently, discussions were held on: (1) The proposal to establish a Farmer Education Center in the Fifth People's Education District was approved in principle. All recurring expenses will be incorporated into the Education Bureau's budget for the 23rd year. (2) Reconsidering the handling of old school site leases upon expiration, it was resolved that all sites would be reclaimed upon expiration. The method of handling the sites will be discussed after reclamation. (3) Regarding whether the bureau's public property located in the Shanghai urban area should be subject to land value tax, it was resolved that the bureau would submit a request to the county, which would then forward it to the municipal government, requesting continued tax exemption based on the original case. (4) Regarding how to establish a contract for the New Puyu Hall's use of the congee distribution factory site, it was resolved that the bureau should establish a formal contract with the hall. (5) Regarding whether the bureau's rental properties in the new county seat should be subject to price reductions in line with the property management office, it was resolved that all properties would be subject to the reduction. (6) The proposal to suspend Sanlin Kindergarten and transfer the original funds to free education was approved as originally proposed. The kindergarten will be suspended from the second semester of this year. From the 23rd year onward, the original funds will be used to establish a primary school between Chenzai and Huanjingxi Songjun townships, with the remaining funds used for repairs and equipment in the fourth district's schools. (7) Designating primary schools to pilot production education (proposed by Yao Huiquan). (8) Determining the education center plan for the 23rd year (proposed by Zhang Yi). The above two proposals were discussed together, and it was resolved to first elect three committee members—Zhu Hange, Yao Huiquan, and Zhang Fengshan—to draft a concrete plan. (9) The proposal to establish education supplies cooperatives by district (proposed by Yao Huiquan) was approved and the Education Bureau will plan the implementation. (10) Regarding the reward and punishment measures for subordinate staff, it was resolved that the Education Bureau should implement them earnestly. (11) The proposal that all unlicensed reed fields identified during the county's land survey should be taken over by the bureau and allocated to education funding was approved. (12) The proposal to promote rural women's education (proposed by Zhang Yi) was approved. From the second semester of the 22nd year, the Education Bureau will designate one or two special people's schools to pilot the program. (13) Designating the leading schools for the third, fourth, fifth, and sixth districts was approved in principle, and the specific measures will be drafted separately. (14) Regarding the request from Huoshan Experimental Township for subsidies for mobile school expenses from February of the 23rd year (proposed by Yao Huiquan), it was resolved that the Education Bureau would allocate 20 yuan per month from the contingency fund and submit a request to the Education Department for approval and implementation.

China Education Construction Actively Implements Production Education

Jointly Organize Production Education with Huangdu Township Teachers' College

The China Education Construction Society, organized by Sun Yuanzeng, Teng Yangyou, Cheng Kuanzheng, Zhang Zhongcui, Wu Zhiqian, and other colleagues in the domestic education sector, aims to promote the production of education. Since the society felt that the Chinese countryside was increasingly bankrupt, it jointly established the Huangdu Chicken Farm with the Huangdu Rural Teachers' College this spring to improve rural sideline occupations and make production education the center of its efforts. The chicken farm is located in Huangdu, where water and land transportation is extremely convenient. It is reported that the construction of the chicken farm and all equipment cost about 2,000 yuan. This year, there are 250 laying hens, and everything is managed according to scientific methods. Experts have also been hired as technicians for the farm. Therefore, the chickens are all strong and lovely. It is reported that the society has resolved to invest another 1,000 yuan each with Huangdu Township Teachers' College next spring to strive for expansion, and plans to set up a chicken farming engineering class and try to raise Chinese chickens, in order to promote the chicken farming business to nearby rural areas and increase farmers' production.

County Education Bureau Director Inspects Education

Shi She, Director of the Shanghai County Education Bureau, in order to assess the educational situation in the county as the first semester of the 22nd year is coming to an end, has been inspecting schools at all levels and social education institutions in various districts for several days. Yesterday morning, Director Shi went to the second district to inspect Yuxiu Daonan and other schools, and Gao Tu also investigated the achievements of mass education. Jinda High School Students Expel Director

(Shen Shi News Agency, local dispatch) All the students of the Affiliated High School of National Jinan University, dissatisfied with the director of the department, Kuang Songling, after the first class, united with more than 100 students from the high school and normal school departments, using steel bedposts as weapons, and forcibly expelled Director Kuang and other faculty and staff, and surrounded and closed the classrooms and offices. The high school department has been completely suspended. President Zheng Hongnian has urgently telegraphed the Ministry of Education twice to report the matter.

Faculty Meeting: After Kuang Songling and the faculty withdrew from the school, they held a meeting with the faculty and staff yesterday afternoon to discuss how to deal with the situation. They all believed that the students' actions were tyrannical and should be severely corrected. It was resolved to ask the president to severely punish them, and if necessary, disband the school, which would not be hesitated.

Kuang Songling's Statement: Yesterday, Kuang Songling told a Shen Shi News Agency reporter that he has been in charge of the school affairs of the Affiliated High School of Jinan University for more than a year, and unfortunately, this kind of turmoil has occurred, which he deeply regrets. However, he has been running schools for many years, and has always advocated strict rectification of the school spirit. Now that a turmoil has occurred in the Affiliated High School of Jinan University and the students are so arrogant, he will never succumb to it. He does not care about his position, and if the students do not realize their mistakes, he and all the faculty and staff will decide to stop teaching, suspend classes, and disband the school from today, which is not enough to talk about rectification. He has already talked about this with President Zheng, who also agrees with him, and believes that if the students still insist, he will take the final step and deal with it strictly.

Telegraph to the Ministry for Instructions: When the turmoil broke out, President Zheng Hongnian, unable to cope with the situation, immediately telegraphed the Ministry of Education in Nanjing to report the truth of the student unrest and request instructions on how to deal with it. Later, at about 4 p.m., he telegraphed the Ministry of Education again to give a detailed account of the student unrest and requested that the students who participated in the unrest be severely punished in order to maintain the school spirit. After the telegram was sent, it is expected that a reply will be received tomorrow, and President Zheng will decide on how to deal with the matter after the Ministry's order arrives.
